href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:urge.html>urge</a>, <a href = </p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>earl</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:earls.html>earls</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:nobility.html>nobility</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:british.html>British</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> Irish <a href = vnd.unilang:nobleman.html>nobleman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:next.html>next</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rank.html>rank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:above.html>above</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> viscount <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:below.html>below</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> marquess; <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:european.html>European</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:count.html>count</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:female.html>female</a> using <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:style.html>style</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> termed <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> countess.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:any.html>Any</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:various.html>various</a> nymphalid butterflies <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genus.html>genus</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Tanaecia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Tanaecia"><i>Tanaecia</i></a></span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:other.html>Other</a> butterflies <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genus.html>genus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:are.html>are</a> called counts <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> viscounts.</li></ol>
